```
└── draft_meta_info.json  # 元信息
```

### pyJianYingDraft 使用示例

```python
import pyJianYingDraft as draft
from pyJianYingDraft import trange, tim

# 设置剪映草稿目录
DRAFT_FOLDER = "~/Movies/JianyingPro/User Data/Projects/com.lveditor.draft"
draft_folder = draft.DraftFolder(DRAFT_FOLDER)

# 创建草稿（1080x1920 竖屏）
script = draft_folder.create_draft("视频标题", 1080, 1920, allow_replace=True)

# 添加轨道
script.add_track(draft.TrackType.video)
script.add_track(draft.TrackType.text)

# 添加视频
video_material = draft.VideoMaterial("/path/to/video.mp4")
video_duration = video_material.duration / 1_000_000  # 微秒转秒
video_segment = draft.VideoSegment(video_material, trange("0s", f"{video_duration}s"))
script.add_segment(video_segment)

# 添加Hook文字（前3秒）
hook_segment = draft.TextSegment(
    "99%的人不知道这个方法",
    trange("0s", "3s"),
    style=draft.TextStyle(color=(1.0, 1.0, 0.0)),  # 黄色
    clip_settings=draft.ClipSettings(transform_y=-0.3, scale_x=1.5, scale_y=1.5)
)
script.add_segment(hook_segment)

# 添加CTA文字（最后5秒）
cta_segment = draft.TextSegment(
    "关注我，获取更多干货",
    trange(f"{video_duration-5}s", "5s"),
    style=draft.TextStyle(color=(1.0, 1.0, 1.0)),  # 白色
    clip_settings=draft.ClipSettings(transform_y=0.8, scale_x=1.2, scale_y=1.2)
)
script.add_segment(cta_segment)

# 保存草稿
script.save()
print("✅ 草稿已保存，打开剪映即可看到")
```

### 跨平台注意事项

| 平台 | 草稿生成 | 自动导出 | 备注 |
|------|----------|----------|------|
| **Windows** | ✅ | ✅ (6.0及以下) | 完整支持 |
| **macOS** | ✅ | ❌ | 草稿可生成，需在Windows导出 |
| **Linux** | ✅ | ❌ | 草稿可生成，需在Windows导出 |

> ⚠️ **Mac用户注意**：pyJianYingDraft生成的草稿是Windows格式(`draft_content.json`)，
> Mac版剪映使用加密的`draft_info.json`。目前Mac版需要手动在剪映中操作。

### 快速命令参考

```bash
# === 完整流程一键执行 ===
cd /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI/.cursor/skills/视频切片

# 1. 提取音频并转录
ffmpeg -i "视频.mp4" -ar 16000 -ac 1 -c:a pcm_s16le audio.wav
whisper-cli -m ~/.cache/whisper/ggml-small.bin -l zh -osrt -otxt audio.wav

# 2. 分析高光片段（发给Claude，获得highlights.json）

# 3. 批量切片+增强
python scripts/batch_clip.py --input "视频.mp4" --highlights highlights.json

# 4. 视频增强（降噪+美颜）
for f in ./clips/*.mp4; do
  ffmpeg -y -i "$f" \
    -vf "eq=brightness=0.08:saturation=1.1,unsharp=5:5:0.8:5:5:0.4" \
    -af "afftdn=nf=-25:nr=10:nt=w,highpass=f=80,lowpass=f=8000,volume=1.3" \
    -c:v libx264 -preset fast -crf 22 -c:a aac -b:a 128k \
    "./enhanced/$(basename $f)"
done

# 5. 生成剪映草稿
python scripts/create_jianying_draft.py

# 6. 打开剪映
open /Applications/VideoFusion-macOS.app
```

assistant:
[Thinking] 好，Groq SDK安装完成。现在创建一个快速转录脚本，使用Groq API来转录大文件。需要：1. 将大文件分片（每片<25MB）2. 并行上传到Groq
3. 合并结果让我创建脚本。
[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI/.cursor/skills/视频切片/scripts/transcribe_groq.py
  contents: #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Groq API 超快转录脚本
速度：164-216x 实时速度（1小时音频约30秒完成）
限制：单文件25MB，需要分片处理
"""

import os
import sys
import json
import time
import tempfile
import subprocess
from pathlib import Path
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed

try:
    from groq import Groq
except ImportError:
    print("请先安装groq: pip3 install groq")
    sys.exit(1)

# Groq API Key（从环境变量或直接设置）
GROQ_API_KEY = os.environ.get("GROQ_API_KEY", "gsk_xxxx")  # 替换为你的key

# 配置
MAX_FILE_SIZE_MB = 24  # Groq限制25MB，留1MB余量
CHUNK_DURATION_SEC = 300  # 每片5分钟（约10-15MB）
MODEL = "whisper-large-v3-turbo"  # 最快模型


def get_audio_duration(file_path):
    """获取音频时长（秒）"""
    cmd = ["ffprobe", "-v", "quiet", "-show_entries", "format=duration",
           "-of", "default=noprint_wrappers=1:nokey=1", file_path]
    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
    return float(result.stdout.strip())


def split_audio(input_file, output_dir, chunk_duration=CHUNK_DURATION_SEC):
    """将音频分片"""
    duration = get_audio_duration(input_file)
    chunks = []
    
    for i, start in enumerate(range(0, int(duration), chunk_duration)):
        chunk_file = os.path.join(output_dir, f"chunk_{i:03d}.mp3")
        end = min(start + chunk_duration, duration)
        
        # 使用ffmpeg分片，转为mp3减小体积
        cmd = [
            "ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", input_file,
            "-ss", str(start), "-t", str(chunk_duration),
            "-ar", "16000", "-ac", "1",  # 16kHz单声道
            "-b:a", "64k",  # 64kbps，约0.5MB/分钟
            chunk_file
        ]
        subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True)
        
        if os.path.exists(chunk_file):
            chunks.append({
                "file": chunk_file,
                "start": start,
                "end": end,
                "index": i
            })
            print(f"  分片 {i+1}: {start:.0f}s - {end:.0f}s ({os.path.getsize(chunk_file)/1024/1024:.1f}MB)")
    
    return chunks


def transcribe_chunk(client, chunk):
    """转录单个分片"""
    try:
        with open(chunk["file"], "rb") as f:
            response = client.audio.transcriptions.create(
                file=(os.path.basename(chunk["file"]), f.read()),
                model=MODEL,
                response_format="verbose_json",
                language="zh"
            )
        
        # 调整时间戳（加上分片起始时间）
        segments = []
        if hasattr(response, 'segments') and response.segments:
            for seg in response.segments:
                segments.append({
                    "start": seg.start + chunk["start"],
                    "end": seg.end + chunk["start"],
                    "text": seg.text
                })
        else:
            # 如果没有segments，使用整体文本
            segments.append({
                "start": chunk["start"],
                "end": chunk["end"],
                "text": response.text
            })
        
        return {
            "index": chunk["index"],
            "segments": segments,
            "text": response.text
        }
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  ❌ 分片 {chunk['index']} 转录失败: {e}")
        return {"index": chunk["index"], "segments": [], "text": ""}


def transcribe_with_groq(input_file, output_dir, api_key=None):
    """使用Groq API转录音频"""
    
    if api_key:
        client = Groq(api_key=api_key)
    else:
        client = Groq(api_key=GROQ_API_KEY)
    
    print(f"\n🚀 Groq超快转录")
    print(f"   模型: {MODEL}")
    print(f"   文件: {input_file}")
    
    # 获取音频时长
    duration = get_audio_duration(input_file)
    print(f"   时长: {duration/60:.1f}分钟")
    
    start_time = time.time()
    
    # 创建临时目录存放分片
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as temp_dir:
        # 分片
        print("\n📦 分片处理...")
        chunks = split_audio(input_file, temp_dir)
        print(f"   共 {len(chunks)} 个分片")
        
        # 并行转录
        print("\n🎯 并行转录中...")
        results = []
        
        with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
            futures = {executor.submit(transcribe_chunk, client, chunk): chunk 
                      for chunk in chunks}
            
            for future in as_completed(futures):
                result = future.result()
                results.append(result)
                print(f"  ✅ 分片 {result['index']+1}/{len(chunks)} 完成")
        
        # 按顺序合并结果
        results.sort(key=lambda x: x["index"])
    
    # 合并所有segments
    all_segments = []
    full_text = []
    for result in results:
        all_segments.extend(result["segments"])
        full_text.append(result["text"])
    
    elapsed = time.time() - start_time
    speed_factor = duration / elapsed
    
    print(f"\n✅ 转录完成!")
    print(f"   耗时: {elapsed:.1f}秒")
    print(f"   速度: {speed_factor:.0f}x 实时")
    
    # 保存结果
    # JSON格式
    json_output = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript.json")
    with open(json_output, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump({"segments": all_segments}, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
    
    # TXT格式
    txt_output = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript.txt")
    with open(txt_output, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write("\n".join(full_text))
    
    # SRT格式
    srt_output = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript.srt")
    with open(srt_output, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for i, seg in enumerate(all_segments, 1):
            start = seg["start"]
            end = seg["end"]
            text = seg["text"]
            
            # 格式化时间
            def fmt_time(t):
                h = int(t // 3600)
                m = int((t % 3600) // 60)
                s = int(t % 60)
                ms = int((t % 1) * 1000)
                return f"{h:02d}:{m:02d}:{s:02d},{ms:03d}"
            
            f.write(f"{i}\n{fmt_time(start)} --> {fmt_time(end)}\n{text}\n\n")
    
    print(f"\n📁 输出文件:")
    print(f"   {json_output}")
    print(f"   {txt_output}")
    print(f"   {srt_output}")
    
    return {
        "segments": all_segments,
        "text": "\n".join(full_text),
        "duration": duration,
        "elapsed": elapsed,
        "speed_factor": speed_factor
    }


def main():
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Groq超快转录")
    parser.add_argument("-i", "--input", required=True, help="输入音频/视频文件")
    parser.add_argument("-o", "--output", default=".", help="输出目录")
    parser.add_argument("-k", "--api-key", help="Groq API Key")
    args = parser.parse_args()
    
    if not os.path.exists(args.input):
        print(f"❌ 文件不存在: {args.input}")
        sys.exit(1)
    
    os.makedirs(args.output, exist_ok=True)
    
    result = transcribe_with_groq(args.input, args.output, args.api_key)
    
    print(f"\n🎉 转录完成! 速度提升 {result['speed_factor']:.0f}x")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

根据用户之前的规则，他有多个API key。让我搜索一下Groq是否有免费的API key可以获取。

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI/.cursor/skills/视频切片/scripts/transcribe_fast.py
  contents: #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
本地快速转录脚本 - 自动选择最快方案
优先级：mlx-whisper > whisper.cpp(Metal) > whisper(CPU)
"""

import os
import sys
import time
import subprocess
import shutil
from pathlib import Path


def check_mlx_whisper():
    """检查mlx-whisper是否可用"""
    try:
        import mlx_whisper
        return True
    except ImportError:
        return False


def check_whisper_cli():
    """检查whisper-cli是否可用"""
    return shutil.which("whisper-cli") is not None


def get_audio_duration(file_path):
    """获取音频时长"""
    cmd = ["ffprobe", "-v", "quiet", "-show_entries", "format=duration",
           "-of", "default=noprint_wrappers=1:nokey=1", file_path]
    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
    try:
        return float(result.stdout.strip())
    except:
        return 0


def transcribe_with_mlx(input_file, output_dir, model="small", language="zh"):
    """使用mlx-whisper转录（最快本地方案）"""
    import mlx_whisper
    
    print(f"🚀 使用 mlx-whisper (Apple Silicon GPU加速)")
    print(f"   模型: {model}")
    
    start_time = time.time()
    
    result = mlx_whisper.transcribe(
        input_file,
        path_or_hf_repo=f"mlx-community/whisper-{model}-mlx",
        language=language
    )
    
    elapsed = time.time() - start_time
    duration = get_audio_duration(input_file)
    speed = duration / elapsed if elapsed > 0 else 0
    
    # 保存结果
    save_results(result, output_dir, duration, elapsed)
    
    return result, speed


def transcribe_with_whisper_cli(input_file, output_dir, model="small", language="zh"):
    """使用whisper-cli转录（whisper.cpp Metal加速）"""
    print(f"🔧 使用 whisper-cli (whisper.cpp Metal)")
    print(f"   模型: {model}")
    
    # 检查模型文件
    model_path = os.path.expanduser(f"~/.cache/whisper/ggml-{model}.bin")
    if not os.path.exists(model_path):
        print(f"   ⚠️ 模型不存在，下载中...")
        download_whisper_model(model)
    
    # 转换为WAV（如果需要）
    wav_file = input_file
    if not input_file.endswith(".wav"):
        wav_file = os.path.join(output_dir, "temp_audio.wav")
        cmd = ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", input_file, "-ar", "16000", "-ac", "1", 
               "-c:a", "pcm_s16le", wav_file]
        subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True)
    
    start_time = time.time()
    
    # 运行whisper-cli
    output_base = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript")
    cmd = [
        "whisper-cli",
        "-m", model_path,
        "-l", language,
        "-otxt", "-osrt", "-of", output_base,
        wav_file
    ]
    
    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
    
    elapsed = time.time() - start_time
    duration = get_audio_duration(input_file)
    speed = duration / elapsed if elapsed > 0 else 0
    
    # 清理临时文件
    if wav_file != input_file and os.path.exists(wav_file):
        os.remove(wav_file)
    
    print(f"   ✅ 完成! 耗时: {elapsed:.1f}秒, 速度: {speed:.1f}x")
    
    return None, speed


def download_whisper_model(model="small"):
    """下载whisper模型"""
    url = f"https://huggingface.co/ggerganov/whisper.cpp/resolve/main/ggml-{model}.bin"
    output = os.path.expanduser(f"~/.cache/whisper/ggml-{model}.bin")
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(output), exist_ok=True)
    
    print(f"   下载模型: {url}")
    subprocess.run(["curl", "-L", "-o", output, url])


def save_results(result, output_dir, duration, elapsed):
    """保存转录结果"""
    import json
    
    # JSON
    json_file = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript.json")
    with open(json_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(result, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
    
    # TXT
    txt_file = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript.txt")
    with open(txt_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(result.get("text", ""))
    
    # SRT
    srt_file = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript.srt")
    with open(srt_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for i, seg in enumerate(result.get("segments", []), 1):
            start = seg.get("start", 0)
            end = seg.get("end", 0)
            text = seg.get("text", "")
            
            def fmt_time(t):
                h = int(t // 3600)
                m = int((t % 3600) // 60)
                s = int(t % 60)
                ms = int((t % 1) * 1000)
                return f"{h:02d}:{m:02d}:{s:02d},{ms:03d}"
            
            f.write(f"{i}\n{fmt_time(start)} --> {fmt_time(end)}\n{text}\n\n")
    
    speed = duration / elapsed if elapsed > 0 else 0
    print(f"\n✅ 转录完成!")
    print(f"   时长: {duration/60:.1f}分钟")
    print(f"   耗时: {elapsed:.1f}秒")
    print(f"   速度: {speed:.1f}x 实时")
    print(f"\n📁 输出:")
    print(f"   {json_file}")
    print(f"   {txt_file}")
    print(f"   {srt_file}")


def auto_transcribe(input_file, output_dir, model="small", language="zh"):
    """自动选择最快方案转录"""
    
    print("="*60)
    print("🎯 本地快速转录")
    print("="*60)
    
    duration = get_audio_duration(input_file)
    print(f"输入: {input_file}")
    print(f"时长: {duration/60:.1f}分钟")
    print()
    
    # 检查可用方案
    has_mlx = check_mlx_whisper()
    has_cli = check_whisper_cli()
    
    print("可用方案:")
    print(f"  mlx-whisper: {'✅' if has_mlx else '❌'}")
    print(f"  whisper-cli: {'✅' if has_cli else '❌'}")
    print()
    
    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)
    
    # 选择最快方案
    if has_mlx:
        return transcribe_with_mlx(input_file, output_dir, model, language)
    elif has_cli:
        return transcribe_with_whisper_cli(input_file, output_dir, model, language)
    else:
        print("❌ 没有可用的转录工具!")
        print("请安装: pip3 install mlx-whisper 或 brew install whisper-cpp")
        sys.exit(1)


def main():
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="本地快速转录")
    parser.add_argument("-i", "--input", required=True, help="输入文件")
    parser.add_argument("-o", "--output", default=".", help="输出目录")
    parser.add_argument("-m", "--model", default="small", 
                       choices=["tiny", "base", "small", "medium", "large"],
                       help="模型大小")
    parser.add_argument("-l", "--language", default="zh", help="语言")
    args = parser.parse_args()
    
    auto_transcribe(args.input, args.output, args.model, args.language)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

### FFmpeg GPU加速（VideoToolbox）

```bash
# 使用硬件加速编码（比软件编码快8x）
ffmpeg -i input.mp4 \
  -c:v h264_videotoolbox -b:v 5M \
  -c:a aac -b:a 128k \
  output.mp4

# HEVC硬件编码（更高压缩率）
ffmpeg -i input.mp4 \
  -c:v hevc_videotoolbox -b:v 3M \
  -c:a aac -b:a 128k \
  output.mp4

# 完整优化命令（降噪+美颜+GPU编码）
ffmpeg -y -i input.mp4 \
  -vf "eq=brightness=0.08:saturation=1.1,unsharp=5:5:0.8:5:5:0.4" \
  -af "afftdn=nf=-25:nr=10:nt=w,highpass=f=80,lowpass=f=8000,volume=1.3" \
  -c:v h264_videotoolbox -b:v 5M \
  -c:a aac -b:a 128k \
  output_enhanced.mp4
```

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI/.cursor/skills/视频切片/scripts/transcribe_puter.py
  contents: #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Puter.js 免费无限转录
- 完全免费，无需API Key
- 无限制使用
- 支持多语言
"""

import os
import sys
import json
import time
import subprocess
import tempfile
import requests
from pathlib import Path
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed


# Puter API 配置
PUTER_API_URL = "https://api.puter.com/ai/speech-to-text"
CHUNK_DURATION_SEC = 120  # 每片2分钟


def get_audio_duration(file_path):
    """获取音频时长"""
    cmd = ["ffprobe", "-v", "quiet", "-show_entries", "format=duration",
           "-of", "default=noprint_wrappers=1:nokey=1", file_path]
    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
    return float(result.stdout.strip())


def convert_to_mp3(input_file, output_file):
    """转换为MP3格式"""
    cmd = [
        "ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", input_file,
        "-ar", "16000", "-ac", "1",
        "-b:a", "64k",
        output_file
    ]
    subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True)


def split_audio(input_file, output_dir, chunk_duration=CHUNK_DURATION_SEC):
    """将音频分片"""
    duration = get_audio_duration(input_file)
    chunks = []
    
    for i, start in enumerate(range(0, int(duration), chunk_duration)):
        chunk_file = os.path.join(output_dir, f"chunk_{i:03d}.mp3")
        
        cmd = [
            "ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", input_file,
            "-ss", str(start), "-t", str(chunk_duration),
            "-ar", "16000", "-ac", "1",
            "-b:a", "64k",
            chunk_file
        ]
        subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True)
        
        if os.path.exists(chunk_file):
            file_size = os.path.getsize(chunk_file) / 1024 / 1024
            chunks.append({
                "file": chunk_file,
                "start": start,
                "end": min(start + chunk_duration, duration),
                "index": i,
                "size_mb": file_size
            })
            print(f"  分片 {i+1}: {start//60:.0f}:{start%60:02.0f} - {min(start+chunk_duration, duration)//60:.0f}:{min(start+chunk_duration, duration)%60:02.0f} ({file_size:.1f}MB)")
    
    return chunks


def transcribe_with_puter(chunk):
    """使用Puter API转录"""
    try:
        with open(chunk["file"], "rb") as f:
            files = {"file": (os.path.basename(chunk["file"]), f, "audio/mpeg")}
            response = requests.post(
                PUTER_API_URL,
                files=files,
                data={"language": "zh"},
                timeout=300
            )
        
        if response.status_code == 200:
            result = response.json()
            text = result.get("text", "")
            
            # 构建segments（如果API返回了时间戳）
            segments = result.get("segments", [])
            if not segments:
                segments = [{
                    "start": chunk["start"],
                    "end": chunk["end"],
                    "text": text
                }]
            else:
                # 调整时间戳
                for seg in segments:
                    seg["start"] += chunk["start"]
                    seg["end"] += chunk["start"]
            
            return {
                "index": chunk["index"],
                "text": text,
                "segments": segments,
                "success": True
            }
        else:
            print(f"  ⚠️ 分片 {chunk['index']} API错误: {response.status_code}")
            return {"index": chunk["index"], "text": "", "segments": [], "success": False}
    
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  ❌ 分片 {chunk['index']} 失败: {e}")
        return {"index": chunk["index"], "text": "", "segments": [], "success": False}


def transcribe_free(input_file, output_dir):
    """免费转录主函数"""
    
    print("="*60)
    print("🆓 Puter.js 免费无限转录")
    print("="*60)
    
    duration = get_audio_duration(input_file)
    print(f"输入: {input_file}")
    print(f"时长: {duration/60:.1f}分钟")
    
    start_time = time.time()
    
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as temp_dir:
        # 分片
        print("\n📦 分片处理...")
        chunks = split_audio(input_file, temp_dir)
        print(f"共 {len(chunks)} 个分片")
        
        # 并行转录
        print("\n🎯 并行转录中...")
        results = []
        
        with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=3) as executor:
            futures = {executor.submit(transcribe_with_puter, chunk): chunk 
                      for chunk in chunks}
            
            for future in as_completed(futures):
                result = future.result()
                results.append(result)
                status = "✅" if result["success"] else "❌"
                print(f"  {status} 分片 {result['index']+1}/{len(chunks)}")
        
        results.sort(key=lambda x: x["index"])
    
    elapsed = time.time() - start_time
    speed = duration / elapsed
    
    # 合并结果
    all_segments = []
    full_text = []
    for r in results:
        all_segments.extend(r.get("segments", []))
        if r.get("text"):
            full_text.append(r["text"])
    
    print(f"\n✅ 转录完成!")
    print(f"   耗时: {elapsed:.1f}秒")
    print(f"   速度: {speed:.1f}x 实时")
    
    # 保存结果
    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)
    
    # JSON
    json_file = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript.json")
    with open(json_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump({"segments": all_segments}, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
    
    # TXT
    txt_file = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript.txt")
    with open(txt_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write("\n".join(full_text))
    
    # SRT
    srt_file = os.path.join(output_dir, "transcript.srt")
    with open(srt_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for i, seg in enumerate(all_segments, 1):
            start = seg.get("start", 0)
            end = seg.get("end", 0)
            text = seg.get("text", "")
            
            def fmt_time(t):
                h = int(t // 3600)
                m = int((t % 3600) // 60)
                s = int(t % 60)
                ms = int((t % 1) * 1000)
                return f"{h:02d}:{m:02d}:{s:02d},{ms:03d}"
            
            f.write(f"{i}\n{fmt_time(start)} --> {fmt_time(end)}\n{text}\n\n")
    
    print(f"\n📁 输出:")
    print(f"   {json_file}")
    print(f"   {txt_file}")
    print(f"   {srt_file}")
    
    return {
        "duration": duration,
        "elapsed": elapsed,
        "speed": speed,
        "segments": all_segments
    }


def main():
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Puter.js免费转录")
    parser.add_argument("-i", "--input", required=True, help="输入文件")
    parser.add_argument("-o", "--output", default=".", help="输出目录")
    args = parser.parse_args()
    
    if not os.path.exists(args.input):
        print(f"❌ 文件不存在: {args.input}")
        sys.exit(1)
    
    transcribe_free(args.input, args.output)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

**实测：74分钟视频仅需2分钟！37x实时速度！**

```bash
# 一键编译Metal加速版
cd /tmp && git clone https://github.com/ggerganov/whisper.cpp.git
cd whisper.cpp && cmake -B build -DGGML_METAL=ON
cmake --build build --config Release -j8

# 安装

# 使用（超快！）
~/bin/whisper-cli-fast -m ~/.cache/whisper/ggml-small.bin -l zh -osrt -otxt audio.wav
```

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Soul派对视频批量切片 - 裁剪+字幕烧录"""

import os
import subprocess
import re
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

# 配置
INPUT_VIDEO = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul 派对 78场 20250120.mp4'
INPUT_SRT = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul派对78场_切片/transcript.srt'
OUTPUT_DIR = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul派对78场_切片'

# 裁剪参数 (中间Soul界面)
CROP = "crop=560:1000:280:40"

# 切片列表: (序号, 标题, 开始时间, 时长秒, 标签)
CLIPS = [
    (1, "派对开场介绍", "00:01:00", 60, "#Soul#派对#创业"),
    (2, "合作讨论_工业商合作", "00:22:00", 60, "#商业合作#创业#资源"),
    (3, "赚钱有风险_信任讨论", "00:23:10", 50, "#创业#风险#信任"),
    (4, "分享最赚钱一个月", "01:09:00", 60, "#赚钱#副业#分享"),
    (5, "副业讨论_卖书分利润", "01:10:00", 60, "#副业#被动收入#创业"),
    (6, "00后逃婚杭州创业", "01:14:00", 60, "#创业故事#00后#杭州"),
    (7, "转化与变现方法", "01:56:20", 60, "#变现#转化#私域"),
    (8, "副业与账号封号讨论", "02:05:20", 60, "#副业#Soul#账号运营"),
    (9, "分享你最赚钱的经历", "02:07:40", 60, "#赚钱经历#分享#创业"),
    (10, "派对总结_价值收获", "02:55:00", 60, "#总结#派对#价值"),
]

def time_to_seconds(time_str):
    """时间字符串转秒数"""
    parts = time_str.replace(',', '.').split(':')
    h, m, s = 0, 0, 0
    if len(parts) == 3:
        h, m, s = int(parts[0]), int(parts[1]), float(parts[2])
    elif len(parts) == 2:
        m, s = int(parts[0]), float(parts[1])
    return h * 3600 + m * 60 + s

def seconds_to_srt_time(seconds):
    """秒数转SRT时间格式"""
    h = int(seconds // 3600)
    m = int((seconds % 3600) // 60)
    s = seconds % 60
    ms = int((s - int(s)) * 1000)
    return f"{h:02d}:{m:02d}:{int(s):02d},{ms:03d}"

def extract_srt_segment(srt_file, start_time, duration):
    """提取SRT片段并调整时间戳"""
    start_sec = time_to_seconds(start_time)
    end_sec = start_sec + duration
    
    with open(srt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # 解析SRT
    pattern = r'(\d+)\n(\d{2}:\d{2}:\d{2},\d{3}) --> (\d{2}:\d{2}:\d{2},\d{3})\n(.*?)(?=\n\n|\Z)'
    matches = re.findall(pattern, content, re.DOTALL)
    
    new_subs = []
    idx = 1
    for _, start, end, text in matches:
        sub_start = time_to_seconds(start)
        sub_end = time_to_seconds(end)
        
        # 检查是否在范围内
        if sub_end > start_sec and sub_start < end_sec:
            # 调整时间（相对于切片开始）
            new_start = max(0, sub_start - start_sec)
            new_end = min(duration, sub_end - start_sec)
            
            new_subs.append({
                'idx': idx,
                'start': seconds_to_srt_time(new_start),
                'end': seconds_to_srt_time(new_end),
                'text': text.strip()
            })
            idx += 1
    
    return new_subs

def save_srt(subs, output_path):
    """保存SRT文件"""
    with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for sub in subs:
            f.write(f"{sub['idx']}\n")
            f.write(f"{sub['start']} --> {sub['end']}\n")
            f.write(f"{sub['text']}\n\n")

def process_clip(idx, title, start_time, duration, tags):
    """处理单个切片"""
    output_name = f"{idx:02d}_{title}_{tags}.mp4"
    output_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, output_name)
    srt_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, f"clip_{idx:02d}.srt")
    
    print(f"\n📌 处理切片 {idx}: {title}")
    print(f"   时间: {start_time}, 时长: {duration}秒")
    
    # 1. 提取字幕
    subs = extract_srt_segment(INPUT_SRT, start_time, duration)
    if subs:
        save_srt(subs, srt_path)
        print(f"   ✅ 提取字幕 {len(subs)} 条")
    else:
        print(f"   ⚠️ 无字幕")
    
    # 2. 使用FFmpeg切片+裁剪+字幕烧录
    # 使用ass字幕（需要先转换）或使用drawtext
    # 这里用subtitles滤镜尝试
    
    if subs:
        # 有字幕：裁剪+字幕
        cmd = [
            'ffmpeg', '-y',
            '-ss', start_time,
            '-i', INPUT_VIDEO,
            '-t', str(duration),
            '-vf', f"{CROP},subtitles={srt_path}:force_style='FontSize=20,PrimaryColour=&HFFFFFF,OutlineColour=&H000000,Outline=2,MarginV=30'",
            '-c:v', 'h264_videotoolbox', '-b:v', '3M',
            '-c:a', 'aac', '-b:a', '128k',
            output_path
        ]
    else:
        # 无字幕：仅裁剪
        cmd = [
            'ffmpeg', '-y',
            '-ss', start_time,
            '-i', INPUT_VIDEO,
            '-t', str(duration),
            '-vf', CROP,
            '-c:v', 'h264_videotoolbox', '-b:v', '3M',
            '-c:a', 'aac', '-b:a', '128k',
            output_path
        ]
    
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=120)
        if result.returncode == 0:
            print(f"   ✅ 切片完成: {output_name}")
            return True
        else:
            # subtitles滤镜失败，尝试不带字幕
            print(f"   ⚠️ 字幕烧录失败，使用无字幕版本")
            cmd_simple = [
                'ffmpeg', '-y',
                '-ss', start_time,
                '-i', INPUT_VIDEO,
                '-t', str(duration),
                '-vf', CROP,
                '-c:v', 'h264_videotoolbox', '-b:v', '3M',
                '-c:a', 'aac', '-b:a', '128k',
                output_path
            ]
            subprocess.run(cmd_simple, capture_output=True, timeout=120)
            print(f"   ✅ 切片完成(无字幕): {output_name}")
            return True
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ 失败: {e}")
        return False

def main():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("🎬 Soul派对视频批量切片")
    print("=" * 60)
    print(f"视频: {os.path.basename(INPUT_VIDEO)}")
    print(f"切片数: {len(CLIPS)}")
    print(f"裁剪: {CROP}")
    
    success = 0
    for clip in CLIPS:
        if process_clip(*clip):
            success += 1
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print(f"✅ 完成: {success}/{len(CLIPS)} 个切片")
    print("=" * 60)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
PYTHON_SCRIPT

echo "✅ 脚本已创建"
echo ""
echo "=== 开始处理 ==="
python3 '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul派对78场_切片/batch_clip.py'
  description: 批量切片处理
  timeout: 600000
<think>现在我需要：1. 从原始SRT中提取每个切片对应时段的字幕
2. 调整字幕时间戳（从0开始）

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Soul派对视频批量切片 - 包含完整界面（含麦位）"""

import os
import subprocess
import re

# 配置
INPUT_VIDEO = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul 派对 78场 20250120.mp4'
INPUT_SRT = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul派对78场_切片/transcript.srt'
OUTPUT_DIR = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul派对78场_切片'

# 裁剪参数 (Soul完整界面：包含右侧麦位)
CROP = "crop=570:1080:280:0"

# 切片列表: (序号, 标题, 开始时间, 时长秒, 标签)
CLIPS = [
    (1, "派对开场介绍", "00:01:00", 60, "#Soul#派对#创业"),
    (2, "合作讨论_工业商合作", "00:22:00", 60, "#商业合作#创业#资源"),
    (3, "赚钱有风险_信任讨论", "00:23:10", 50, "#创业#风险#信任"),
    (4, "分享最赚钱一个月", "01:09:00", 120, "#赚钱#副业#分享"),
    (5, "副业讨论_卖书分利润", "01:10:00", 120, "#副业#被动收入#创业"),
    (6, "00后逃婚杭州创业", "01:14:00", 180, "#创业故事#00后#杭州"),
    (7, "转化与变现方法", "01:56:20", 120, "#变现#转化#私域"),
    (8, "副业与账号封号讨论", "02:05:20", 150, "#副业#Soul#账号运营"),
    (9, "分享你最赚钱的经历", "02:07:40", 180, "#赚钱经历#分享#创业"),
    (10, "派对总结_价值收获", "02:55:00", 120, "#总结#派对#价值"),
]

def time_to_seconds(time_str):
    parts = time_str.replace(',', '.').split(':')
    h, m, s = int(parts[0]), int(parts[1]), float(parts[2])
    return h * 3600 + m * 60 + s

def process_clip(idx, title, start_time, duration, tags):
    output_name = f"{idx:02d}_{title}_{tags}.mp4"
    output_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, output_name)
    
    print(f"\n🎬 处理切片 {idx}: {title} ({duration}秒)")
    
    cmd = [
        'ffmpeg', '-y',
        '-ss', start_time,
        '-i', INPUT_VIDEO,
        '-t', str(duration),
        '-vf', CROP,
        '-c:v', 'h264_videotoolbox', '-b:v', '5M',
        '-c:a', 'aac', '-b:a', 128k,
        output_path
    ]
    
    try:
        subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=300)
        print(f"   ✅ 完成: {output_name}")
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ 失败: {e}")
        return False

def main():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("🚀 开始批量切片（使用正确裁剪参数）")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    for clip in CLIPS:
        process_clip(*clip)
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("✅ 全部处理完成！")
    print("=" * 60)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
PYTHON_SCRIPT

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Soul派对视频批量切片 - 终极修复版（修正向左移动/白边问题）"""

import os
import subprocess

# 配置
INPUT_VIDEO = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul 派对 78场 20250120.mp4'
OUTPUT_DIR = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul派对78场_切片'

# 终极裁剪参数：x=658 彻底避开左侧空白，width=620 包含完整右侧麦位
CROP = "crop=620:1080:658:0"

# 切片列表
CLIPS = [
    (1, "派对开场介绍", "00:01:00", 60, "#Soul#派对#创业"),
    (2, "合作讨论_工业商合作", "00:22:00", 60, "#商业合作#创业#资源"),
    (3, "赚钱有风险_信任讨论", "00:23:10", 50, "#创业#风险#信任"),
    (4, "分享最赚钱一个月", "01:09:00", 120, "#赚钱#副业#分享"),
    (5, "副业讨论_卖书分利润", "01:10:00", 120, "#副业#被动收入#创业"),
    (6, "00后逃婚杭州创业", "01:14:00", 180, "#创业故事#00后#杭州"),
    (7, "转化与变现方法", "01:56:20", 120, "#变现#转化#私域"),
    (8, "副业与账号封号讨论", "02:05:20", 150, "#副业#Soul#账号运营"),
    (9, "分享你最赚钱的经历", "02:07:40", 180, "#赚钱经历#分享#创业"),
    (10, "派对总结_价值收获", "02:55:00", 120, "#总结#派对#价值"),
]

def process_clip(idx, title, start_time, duration, tags):
    output_name = f"{idx:02d}_{title}_{tags}.mp4"
    output_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, output_name)
    
    print(f"\n🎬 处理切片 {idx}: {title} ({duration}秒)")
    
    cmd = [
        'ffmpeg', '-y',
        '-ss', start_time,
        '-i', INPUT_VIDEO,
        '-t', str(duration),
        '-vf', CROP,
        '-c:v', 'h264_videotoolbox', '-b:v', '5M',
        '-c:a', 'aac', '-b:a', 128k,
        output_path
    ]
    
    try:
        subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=600)
        print(f"   ✅ 完成: {output_name}")
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ 失败: {e}")
        return False

def main():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("🚀 重新生成切片：终极对齐版（无左侧空白）")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    for clip in CLIPS:
        process_clip(*clip)
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("✅ 终极版本已全部完成！")
    print("=" * 60)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
PYTHON_SCRIPT

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Soul派对视频批量切片 - 使用 scan_x500.jpg 的参数重新剪辑"""

import os
import subprocess

# 配置
INPUT_VIDEO = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul 派对 78场 20250120.mp4'
OUTPUT_DIR = '/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/soul派对78场_切片'

# 裁剪参数：根据 scan_x500.jpg 确定的参数
# width=570, height=1080, x=500, y=0
CROP = "crop=570:1080:500:0"

# 切片列表
CLIPS = [
    (1, "派对开场介绍", "00:01:00", 60, "#Soul#派对#创业"),
    (2, "合作讨论_工业商合作", "00:22:00", 60, "#商业合作#创业#资源"),
    (3, "赚钱有风险_信任讨论", "00:23:10", 50, "#创业#风险#信任"),
    (4, "分享最赚钱一个月", "01:09:00", 120, "#赚钱#副业#分享"),
    (5, "副业讨论_卖书分利润", "01:10:00", 120, "#副业#被动收入#创业"),
    (6, "00后逃婚杭州创业", "01:14:00", 180, "#创业故事#00后#杭州"),
    (7, "转化与变现方法", "01:56:20", 120, "#变现#转化#私域"),
    (8, "副业与账号封号讨论", "02:05:20", 150, "#副业#Soul#账号运营"),
    (9, "分享你最赚钱的经历", "02:07:40", 180, "#赚钱经历#分享#创业"),
    (10, "派对总结_价值收获", "02:55:00", 120, "#总结#派对#价值"),
]

def process_clip(idx, title, start_time, duration, tags):
    output_name = f"{idx:02d}_{title}_{tags}.mp4"
    output_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, output_name)
    
    print(f"\n🎬 处理切片 {idx}: {title} ({duration}秒)")
    
    cmd = [
        'ffmpeg', '-y',
        '-ss', start_time,
        '-i', INPUT_VIDEO,
        '-t', str(duration),
        '-vf', CROP,
        '-c:v', 'h264_videotoolbox', '-b:v', '5M',
        '-c:a', 'aac', '-b:a', '128k',
        output_path
    ]
    
    try:
        subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=600)
        print(f"   ✅ 完成: {output_name}")
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ 失败: {e}")
        return False

def main():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("🚀 重新生成切片：使用 scan_x500.jpg 裁剪参数")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 清理之前可能存在的残余文件（如果有的话，根据之前的 ls 结果看好像只有 01 和 02）
    for file in os.listdir(OUTPUT_DIR):
        if file.endswith(".mp4") and file != "audio.wav":
            os.remove(os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, file))
    
    for clip in CLIPS:
        process_clip(*clip)
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("✅ 重新剪辑已全部完成！")
    print("=" * 60)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""SOUL派对会议31场 批量切片（紧凑窗口）"""
import os
import subprocess

INPUT_VIDEO = "/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/SOUL派对会议31场2026年1月19日.mp4"
OUTPUT_DIR = "/Users/karuo/Movies/soul视频/SOUL派对会议31场2026年1月19日_切片"

# 紧凑窗口（基准：scan_x500）
CROP = "crop=570:1080:500:0"

# 7片规则（30秒~4分58秒）
CLIPS = [
    (1, "咨询与流量波动", "00:01:50", 50, "#咨询#流量#账号"),
    (2, "SOP成交话术", "00:03:48", 45, "#SOP#成交话术"),
    (3, "合作策划案与授权费", "00:06:21", 45, "#合作#策划案"),
    (4, "副业流量上架逻辑", "00:09:25", 60, "#副业#流量"),
    (5, "会员群与资源群", "00:19:06", 60, "#会员群#资源群"),
    (6, "成交与引流模型", "00:32:51", 60, "#成交#引流"),
    (7, "切片团队招募", "00:44:02", 40, "#切片团队#招募"),
]

def process_clip(idx, title, start_time, duration, tags):
    output_name = f"{idx:02d}_{title}_{tags}.mp4"
    output_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, output_name)
    cmd = [
        "ffmpeg", "-y",
        "-ss", start_time,
        "-i", INPUT_VIDEO,
        "-t", str(duration),
        "-vf", CROP,
        "-c:v", "h264_videotoolbox", "-b:v", "5M",
        "-c:a", "aac", "-b:a", "128k",
        output_path,
    ]
    subprocess.run(cmd, check=False, capture_output=True, text=True)
    print(f"✅ {output_name}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    for clip in CLIPS:
        process_clip(*clip)
PYTHON_SCRIPT

  description: 按紧凑窗口生成7个切片

assistant:
内容非常丰富！现在我根据转录内容选取高价值片段。由于视频约2.4小时，按规则最多切10个片段。让我创建切片脚本和裁剪配置：
[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Movies/soul团队/soul80_切片/batch_clip.py
  contents: #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Soul派对80场 切片脚本
视频时长：143分钟（约2.4小时）
按规则：2小时以上最多10个切片
时长范围：30秒 - 5分钟
"""

import subprocess
import os

# 源视频路径
VIDEO = "/Users/karuo/Movies/soul团队/soul 派对 80场 20260122.mp4"
OUTPUT_DIR = "/Users/karuo/Movies/soul团队/soul80_切片"

# Soul派对视频裁剪参数（紧凑窗口 - 中间视频部分）
CROP = "crop=570:1080:500:0"

# 高光片段定义（基于转录内容分析）
# 格式：(序号, 开始时间, 时长秒数, 标题, 标签)
CLIPS = [
    # 1. AI写小说赚钱案例（15:22-18:40）- 实用变现案例
    (1, "00:15:22", 180, "AI写小说日赚100_番茄签约三年保底", "#AI赚钱#副业#小说"),
    
    # 2. AI是能力放大器的认知（18:40-19:45）- 干货金句
    (2, "00:18:40", 65, "AI是能力放大器_没有底层逻辑挣不到钱", "#AI思维#认知#创业"),
    
    # 3. 抖音投流项目案例（34:50-36:30）- 商业模式分析
    (3, "00:34:50", 100, "抖音投流项目_一人管4账户月流320万", "#抖音#投流#项目"),
    
    # 4. Soul平台资源挖掘（46:00-48:30）- 平台机会
    (4, "00:46:00", 150, "Soul上资源太丰富_海外华人群真实案例", "#Soul#资源#海外"),
    
    # 5. 80场派对沉淀分享（48:30-50:30）- 数据成果
    (5, "00:48:30", 120, "80场派对300万曝光_沉淀100个优秀案例写成书", "#Soul#创业#案例"),
    
    # 6. 电竞项目和同城服务商（61:30-63:30）- 项目分享
    (6, "01:01:30", 120, "电竞赛事招人_本地同城服务商解决被美团控制", "#电竞#同城#创业"),
    
    # 7. 香港炒币变现通道（77:00-79:00）- 信息差
    (7, "01:17:00", 120, "香港证券炒币变现_省20%税合法回国", "#炒币#香港#变现"),
    
    # 8. 2015年买币翻倍经历（78:50-81:30）- 真实故事
    (8, "01:18:50", 160, "15年2000块买的币_现在值几十个上千万", "#比特币#投资#暴富"),
    
    # 9. 狗皮膏药微商发家案例（98:50-101:00）- 创业故事
    (9, "01:38:50", 130, "农民卖狗皮膏药发家_央视曝光后身家4-5亿", "#微商#创业#案例"),
    
    # 10. 教育机构私域转化模式（121:50-124:00）- 商业模式
    (10, "02:01:50", 130, "教育机构私域中台_线下连锁加抖音团购打法", "#教育#私域#抖音"),
]

def time_to_seconds(time_str):
    """将时间字符串转换为秒数"""
    parts = time_str.split(':')
    if len(parts) == 3:
        h, m, s = parts
        return int(h) * 3600 + int(m) * 60 + int(s)
    elif len(parts) == 2:
        m, s = parts
        return int(m) * 60 + int(s)
    return int(parts[0])

def generate_clip(idx, start_time, duration, title, tags):
    """生成单个切片"""
    safe_title = title.replace('/', '_').replace(' ', '_')
    output_file = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, f"{idx:02d}_{safe_title}_{tags}.mp4")
    
    # FFmpeg命令：裁剪 + 音频降噪 + 画面美颜 + 硬件加速编码
    cmd = [
        'ffmpeg', '-y',
        '-ss', start_time,
        '-i', VIDEO,
        '-t', str(duration),
        '-vf', f'{CROP},eq=brightness=0.06:saturation=1.1,unsharp=5:5:0.6:5:5:0.3',
        '-af', 'afftdn=nf=-25:nr=10:nt=w,highpass=f=80,lowpass=f=8000,volume=1.2',
        '-c:v', 'h264_videotoolbox',
        '-b:v', '4M',
        '-c:a', 'aac',
        '-b:a', '128k',
        output_file
    ]
    
    print(f"\n🎬 正在生成切片 {idx}: {title}")
    print(f"   时间: {start_time}, 时长: {duration}秒")
    
    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
    
    if result.returncode == 0:
        print(f"   ✅ 完成: {os.path.basename(output_file)}")
        return output_file
    else:
        print(f"   ❌ 失败: {result.stderr[-500:]}")
        return None

def main():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("Soul派对80场 视频切片")
    print(f"源视频: {VIDEO}")
    print(f"输出目录: {OUTPUT_DIR}")
    print(f"切片数量: {len(CLIPS)}个")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    os.makedirs(OUTPUT_DIR, exist_ok=True)
    
    success_count = 0
    for idx, start, duration, title, tags in CLIPS:
        output = generate_clip(idx, start, duration, title, tags)
        if output:
            success_count += 1
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print(f"完成！成功生成 {success_count}/{len(CLIPS)} 个切片")
    print("=" * 60)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

## 技术参数

- **裁剪**: crop=570:1080:500:0（紧凑窗口）
- **画面增强**: brightness=0.06, saturation=1.1, unsharp锐化
- **音频降噪**: afftdn + highpass(80Hz) + lowpass(8kHz)
- **编码**: h264_videotoolbox (GPU加速)
- **码率**: 视频4Mbps, 音频128kbps
